DROP TABLE Food;
CREATE TABLE Food(
  FoodId         NUMBER(5)     NOT NULL,
  Name           VARCHAR(100)  NOT NULL,
  Description    VARCHAR(350),
  Status         VARCHAR(10)   NOT NULL,
PRIMARY KEY (FoodId),
CONSTRAINT chk_status_f CHECK (Status in ('Active', 'Inactive'))
);
